For about maybe 30 years of being a school bus driver for M.P.U.S.D I had the pleasure of participating in the Big Sur International marathon. Also my father Cecil Brown volunteered as well. may he rest in peace. When I was a bus driver, we would have breakfast at this restaurant. I am retired now but I will never forget the hospitality of this establishment to us every year. my specialty would be they're chicken fried steak with sausage gravy. My former fellow bus drivers will be there Sunday morning 4-24-16 as usual every year in the morning. We would all Gather in one bus and travel down the road not too far to enjoy a good hot breakfast. I will not forget their Hospitality to us. And I will pass the word that even though i may not be there participating driving for the marathon, I will miss they'e chicken fried steak with sausage gravy. Being a foodie myself, if anybody reads this try their chicken fried steak. you can have it with eggs pancakes or whatever it is worth it.<//review>

<UserId.>113289238139906248100< /UserId.><Date>1516076457556< /Date><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< review>
I've eaten at a thousand or more Mexican restaurants in my life......seriously! and I stumbled across this place today, only because I googled another place but it didn't exist. Anyway it is a stand up order place, then they bring you your food into a dining area that would rival any well thought out sit down restaurant. The salsa for our chips was very fresh and amazing,  so I should have known what was to come........My son and his friend ordered a burrito and a chimichanga, they were huge, I haven't seen a burrito that big in years and they loved it. I ordered a street taco combo plate, with Pastor (spicy pork) rice and beans, hands down the best pastor ever in my life, on my dumb luck find. This place is really really good. I'm not plugging this place and I promise you it deserves your business, but only if you want to be blown away like I was. Thank you El Taco De Guadalajara, I'll be back and spread the good word!< /review>

<user_id>111000681920634031171<//user_id><username>David Jeffrey<//username><Date>1466384807320< /Date><Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
We were driving around look for a hole in the wall restaurant and so glad we stumbled onto this place. By far the best Mexican food I have had in Ventura or Thousand Oaks. This is a family owned business and everyone is very friendly. I agree the service is a little slow but the food more than makes up for it.
It's a family run, small mom and pop business working their butts off trying to do the best they can.
I've been to some of the high-end Mexican restaurants in the city and Thousand Oaks and none of them come close to the food, huge portions, and low prices this little gem offers.
It's really sad and unfair to read so many harsh reviews about this place. This is why we end up with so many fast food restaurants and great family owned businesses like this are far and few between.</text>

< Review>
Discovered this place earlier this week after tracking down the new address of the old taco de Mexico that used to be next to the mall.  I was happy to see that the prices were affordable and ordered my standard Chile relleno burrito.  While it was being prepared, I dove in to the chips and found that the salsa bar was chock full of delicious yet spicy salsa... Just as it should be at a Mexican food restaurant.

When our food arrived,  we were just as satisfied and left feeling very full as the burritos are huge.  I've been here twice since then and have enjoyed it just as much both times.  Glad we have a great Mexican food place in mid town and I'm looking forward to coming back.<//Review>

< text>
A few general comments:
- Service is fast, but not great
- Portion size is large
- Too many posters with specials
- "Chupacabra" meat selection is non-standard. Server had to ask cook what was in it.
- Price to quality was too high; volume doesn't make up for flavor

Food comments:
- Huge portions
- Very oversalted meat
- No salt on chips
- Low salt in refried beans
- Salsa red and green were very tasty
- Barbacoa taco was tasty

Overall, a middling food effort. If you want better food go to just about any place on Ventura Avenue; however, will suffice if you live local and don't want to drive an extra 10min.< /text>

We had a really pleasant shopping experience during the Black Friday Sales event. Gary, the sales person was very patient and helpful. He allowed us to roam around the whole store and explore, while answering all of our questions in regards color schemes and pairings available. This is probably one of very few furniture/home furnishing stores where sales reps do not hover over your head and try to persuade you to make a purchase immediately. Needless to say, the furniture at Scandinavian Designs sells itself and once you try out some of the pieces you will want to own all of them. We selected a couple of electronically reclining couches for our new living room, as well as a media center, a full set of side tables, a rug and two giant oil paintings to tie it all together, as well as a dining table and 6 chair set. They should be delivered this week and we will update the review once delivery takes place and we have a chance to use and enjoy our new furniture. It's rare to find things on sale at Scandinavian Designs and we wanted to capitalize on the opportunity to own some really nice high end pieces. We will come back when we need to remodel the bedrooms as there were some very modern and appealing sets available, but our budget was already maxed out.</Review>

Quality of products- ZERO (the majority of furniture is beaten and battered)
Customer Service rating- ZERO (Lin quite obviously dislikes his job as well as the customers, I will expand more on this in a moment.

Purchased a painting. When we got it home we found that due to the packaging by Scandinavian Design all 4 corners were damaged beyond repair. We were told to come back for an exchange. We asked to look at the new painting before we took it home and it was in worse condition than the first one. Not to mention that the colors were completely different. The warehouse guys told us that they had just received a new shipment of paintings and that we should look in the showroom for a replacement. We found 2 painting and a mirror. We were told by Lin that we could not purchase the mirror and that we have to order the paintings! We explained our concerns regarding quality (or lack there of) and the inability of guaranteeing that the colors would be exactly the same. It's a painting not a print. How can you possibly purchase something that's going to be a focal point on your wall sight unseen? Not to mention the waisted time on our part driving back and forth with the trailer. He (Lin) absolutely refused to understand or care, nor did he do a good job of disguising his distain. So instead of purchasing 4 pieces of art we walked out. I will also add that the manager was lurking behind him during the entire exchange. Apparently conflict resolution, customer service or even a positive disposition are not needed when seeking employment with this company.< /review>

<gmapID>0x80857dd22a1ca3cb:0x83023f2c87a960f5<//gmapID>< review>
*FRAUD alert. I recently moved to the area and have visited twice; once for a routine cleaning and second to have my wisdom teeth extracted and a deep cleaning performed. Actual dental care was great; spectacular customer service,w ith qualified and efficient dental professionals serving you.  Careful, patient, and kind dental hygiene specialists..

However, I inadvertently left my debit card at their office the date of my second (and last) appointment. I was called that they had my card in their possession; a staff member later informed me that she would send the card to my home along with a statement. When I received the statement and my card, it was debited an ADDITIONAL $500, on the date that THEIR DENTAL OFFICE HAD POSSESSION OF MY CARD, in an UNAUTHORIZED TRANSACTION for which no notice was provided, nor consent granted. No phone call informing me that they had reassessed a fee, no request to charge an additional amount, no apology about a discrepancy, and absolutely no authorization before charging my DEBIT account an additional $500 at their own liberty. I can only imagine this occurring to people with actual financial issues, including the ramifications of overdraft fees, etc.

The administrative staff must make a habit of this, as I sent an email to the dental office requesting a fee estimate two weeks prior to the appointment, no response; called in personally, was quoted ~$180; was again quoted and charged ~$180 before leaving my appointment, yet they informed me after pointing out the discrepancy that "they did not know where the $180 figure came from but that the charge was incorrect so they fixed it."

This was no mistake of theirs, and they deliberately (and fraudulently) decided to take it within their own liberty to charge my account whatever "amount they desired" without consulting me personally. This is egregious conduct that, if systemic, should be immediately reported to the proper city authorities. I highly recommend that past customers, especially those using Health Savings Accounts or other similar benefits through employers, take a look at their balances for hidden charges that vary from the actual receipt which they signed. In my case, I have both receipts and voicemails from staff members both before and after the date of the charges indicating that I did not have possession (nor did i sign any paper authorizing the charge), thus proving the lack of consent to the charges assessed. Luckily, the difference was not extreme, but the fact that it was effectuated without my permission makes this instance, no matter how isolated, a deeply intolerable incident.< /review>
